  197. How do you compare the hundreds of skin care products? As a regular tester, I've arrived at a list of key considerations. I hope these help you!<br /><br />~ Fragrance: Virtually none<br />~ Feel during application: Like a nice medium-weight moisturizing lotion. Not oily, but certainly emollient.<br />~ Feel after absorption: My VERY sensitive skin feels a very slight warmth, but nothing close to the unpleasant experience I’ve had with some other retinol creams. Running fingers across skin, you can feel it, halfway between oily and sticky, but neither. This isn’t the unpleasant film some lotions leave, and the skin feels moisturized. This DID irritate my eyes when I applied a little too close to them and later rubbed my eyes. Keep away from eyes actually applies here.<br />~ Is it best for a certain skin type?: I think it should be fine for all of them.<br />~ Is it tested on animals?: No.<br />~ Packaging: 3.4oz broad pump-top plastic bottle with cap. The pump is precise and easy to use. Bottle size is generous enough to use on hands and neck as well as face. Note that mine had a pink label, not the black shown in current photos.<br />~ Immediate cosmetic effects:* If your skin was a bit in need of a moisturizer, this will brighten it up and reduce the appearance of fine lines.<br />~ Potential long-term effectiveness:* Retinol is a superb anti-aging ingredient and will absolutely make your skin look better. My problem has always been finding a retinol cream that wasn’t sticky and didn’t flush my skin, so I’m very happy with this one. Hyaluronic acid is another good long-term ingredient, and the moisturizers (aloe, shea butter, and glycerin) in it are good. If you don’t yet use a retinol cream, you are missing something and this would be a good one to try.<br /><br />*Know the difference between cosmetic and long-term effects: Cosmetic effects are immediate and only present when the product has been applied recently - just like makeup. Long-term effects take longer to see and should remain when you stop using the product (but don't when you find something effective - your skin needs continuing support). The ideal product would be both cosmetically and long-term effective, but it's more realistic to expect a formula to tilt towards one or the other.<br /><br />I received this free or virtually so for product testing and review.
